UML Conventions Comformance Report

[ 20/05/2020 ]

Publications Office of the European Union
Luxembourg
https://op.europa.eu

Abstract

eProcurement UML model needs to conform to a set of UML conventions described elsewhere. A conformance checking script was developed to execute tests to the UML model and generate errors or warnings when encountered.

This document was automatically generated by the conformance checking script and comprises the UML conformance violations.

The organisation of this document is based on major types of UML elements and connectors that are employed in the eProcurement conceptual model. They are as follows: Classes, Enumerations, Datatypes, Packages, Associations, Dependencies and Generalisations. Each major section lists model items that need correction of errors or consideration of warnings.

The UML model in file ePO-CM-v2.0.2-2020-05-19.eap.xmi was tested at 09:43 on May 20, 2020.

Classes

Amount

Unmet class conventions
The name of element Amount is missing a prefix. The name should comprise a prefix respecing the syntax prefix:localSegment.
The name prefix , is invalid. Please provide a short prefix name containing only alphanumeric characters [a-zA-Z0-9]+.
The name Amount is not unique. The Concept names should be unique within the model; while the relations may repeat but should not overlap with concept names.
The class Amount has no attributes provided. A class should define some attributes.
Amount is missing a description. All concepts should be defined or described.
The name Amount does not match the pattern. The name should respect the syntax prefix:localSegment (similar to the XML QName).
The prefix is not defined. A prefix must be associated to a namespace URI.
